izlude,103,106,3	script	Guildsman#1	48,3,3,{

	if(checkweight(7416,1) != 1)
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ^3355FFWait a second!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Right now, you're carrying";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] too many things with you.";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Please come back after";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] using the Kafra Service";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to store some of your items.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if(!(BaseLevel > 59) || !(BaseJob == Job_Novice || BaseJob == Job_Super_Novice || BaseClass == Job_Swordman))
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] There are rumors";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] going around about";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] the disappearances of";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] children in the Morroc";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] area. Some guilds believe";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] these are actually kidnappings.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Those poor kids...";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] If I could do something";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to help them, by George,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] I would do it in a flash.";
		close;
	}
	if(!mao_request)
	{
		if ((BaseJob == Job_Novice) || (BaseJob == Job_Super_Novice))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "Excuse me? "+strcharinfo(0)+"?";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Hi there, I've been waiting for";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you to wander past me for such";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] a long time, you know that?";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Novices and Super Novices";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] are so hard to track down...";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Anyway, I don't know if you";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] know this, but a lot of kids are missing from Morroc recently.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] We're not sure, but we think it's related to the latest assignment";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] for our Assassin Guild.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Anyway, the client for this";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] assignment needs all the help";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] he can get. Now, I've heard";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] about you, and I think that";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you could be really helpful to";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] us in this specific situation.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Look, just do me a favor";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] and do the right thing like";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you always do, okay? Here's";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] a letter of recommendation";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] to get you started on this";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] mission, alright?";
			set mao_request,1;
			getitem 7416,1;
			close;
		}
		else if((BaseJob == Job_Swordman) || (BaseJob == Job_Swordman_High))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "Hey, " + strcharinfo(0) + "!";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Great, I knew you'd";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] show up sooner or later.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Listen, I'm working here";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] as a representative of the";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Swordman Assocation.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Listen, there's something";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] big going on, and I think it's";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] the most important thing the";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Swordman Association has ever";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] been involved in. Pack your bags and head to Morroc right now!";
			next;
			mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] All the way to Morroc...?";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Why, what's going on?";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I don't know all the details,";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] but the Assassin Guild is";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] working on some missing";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] children's case, and they've";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] requested help from us and";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] all the other guilds...";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Rogues, Bards, Novices,";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Super Novices, Priests...";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] You name it. This is gonna be";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] huge. Listen, if you're going";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] to help, then let me give you this letter of recommendation...";
			set mao_request,1;
			getitem 7416,1;
			close;
		}
		else if((Class == Job_Knight) || (Class == Job_Lord_Knight))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "" + strcharinfo(0) +"...?";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I knew you'd show up if";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Listen, I have a notice for";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you from the Prontera Chivalry.";
			next;
			mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] For me? That sounds";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] strange, but would you";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] please read it to me?";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "''RE: "+ strcharinfo(0) +"";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] As leader of the Prontera";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Chivalry, I formally request";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you to represent the Knights of";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Rune-Midgarts in cooperation";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] with the Assassin Guild.''";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Please assist the Assassin";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Guild in any way befitting of";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] the Knighthood in a special";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] mission to rescue children";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] missing from Morroc.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] -- Captain Herman''";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] There, that's all it says.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Here, I think you'll need";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] this letter of recommendation";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] if you plan to follow these";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] orders. I hope you take that";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] mission for those kids' sake...";
			set mao_request,1;
			getitem 7416,1;
			close;
		}
		else if((Class == Job_Crusader) || (Class == Job_Paladin))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Excuse me...?";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...?";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I'm sorry to bother you, but";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I've got an urgent communique";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] for you from Sir Michael Halig";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] of the Crusaders...";
			next;
			mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] They usually don't";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] send messages. I guess";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] whatever he has to say";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] must be really important.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] What does it say?";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Let's see here... Something";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] about a missing children's case";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] the the Assassin Guild is working on... Ah! The Assassin Guild has";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] requested help from the Crusaders. So I guess you were recommended.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Look, here's the letter of";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] recommendation that I'm";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] supposed to give you if you";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] plan on taking the mission.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] For the sake of those missing kids, I really hope that you do.";
			set mao_request,1;
			getitem 7416,1;
			close;
		}
	}
	else if(mao_request == 1)
	{
		if ((BaseJob == Job_Novice) || (BaseJob == Job_Super_Novice))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Ah, I forgot to tell you";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] exactly where you need to";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] go for the mission details!";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Let's see... You're supposed";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] to... Ah, now I remember~";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] If you check out the";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] west side of the Oasis";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] inside Morroc, you'll find";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] a very suspicious looking";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] hut. Your contact from the";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Assassin Guild is near there.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I'm sure you'll find it if";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you keep your eyes open.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Anyway, that's all I know.";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Why don't you go check it out?";
			close;
		}
		else if((BaseJob == Job_Swordman) || (BaseJob == Job_Swordman_High))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Right, for this mission,";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] you'll need to meet with your";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] contact from the Assassin";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Guild near a hut at the west";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] side of the Oasis inside Morroc. So keep an eye out for him.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I doubt you'll have";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] trouble finding the guy,";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] even if all Thieves and";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Assassins are starting";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] to look the same. You";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] know what I mean, right?";
			close;
		}
		else if((Class == Job_Knight) || (Class == Job_Lord_Knight) || (Class == Job_Crusader) || (Class == Job_Paladin))
		{
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Are you thinking of taking";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] the mission? That's great!";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Now, you need to meet your";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] contact from the Assassin";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] Guild outside a hut on the west side of the Oasis inside Morroc.";
			next;
			mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] I know those directions";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] aren't very clear, but this";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] is supposedly a top secret";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] location that's usually only";
			mes "[DRY-RUN] known to the Assassins...";
			close;
		}
	}
	else if(((mao_request > 2) && (mao_request < 27)) || ((mao_request > 102) && (mao_request < 125)))
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] It looks like you're";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] working well with the";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Assassin Guild. Still,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] be careful. There might";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] be more to this mission";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] than meets the eye, you know?";
		close;
	}
	else
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Guildsman]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] It's a nice day, isn't it?";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Though, I hope something";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] exciting happens soon. Peace";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] is great and all, but I prefer";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to have my life shook up";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] every now and then.";
		close;
	}

OnTouch:
	if(checkweight(7416,1) != 1)
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ^3355FFWait a second!";

		mes "[DRY-RUN] Please come back after";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] using the Kafra Service";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to store some of your items.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if(BaseLevel > 59)
	{
		if(!mao_request)

prontera,237,313,3	script	Nun#moc	79,3,3,{

	if(checkweight(7416,1) != 1)
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ^3355FFWait a second!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Right now, you're carrying";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] too many things with you.";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Please come back after";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] using the Kafra Service";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to store some of your items.^000000";
		close;
	}
	if(!(BaseLevel > 59))
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Oh, hello there~";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Peace be with you,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] adventurer. Remember";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] that no matter how different";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] people may be, all of us are";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] united in our humanity.";
		close;
	}
	if(!(BaseClass == Job_Acolyte))
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Ah, hello. Would you ask";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] anyone that you know";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to be affiliated with the";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Prontera Church to talk to";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] me? Acolytes, Priests, Monks...";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Any of those would be fine.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] I have something very";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] important to tell them,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] but it's almost impossible";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to gather all the clergy";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] in an emergency situation...";
		close;
	}
	if(!mao_request)
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "Oh, " + strcharinfo(0) + "!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] It must be an act of";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] divine providence that";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] we finally meet. Actually,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] I have something very";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] important to ask you.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] You may have heard that";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] there's been a recent influx";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] of missing child reports from";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Morroc. Apparently, someone";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] has hired the Assassin Guild";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to investigate these cases.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Since this is such a huge";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] issue, the Assassin Guild has";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] even gone so far as to request";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] the Prontera Church for help, so I'd like you to aid the Assassin";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Guild in this mission.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] However, I believe that";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] the Assassin Guild's client";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] may have other intentions,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] so I also want you to keep";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] an eye out and see if their";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] client can be trusted.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Nun]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Please visit Morroc";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] as soon as you can.";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] When you arrive, you";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] will need the Bishop's";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] letter of recommendation,";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] so please take it now.";
		set mao_request,1;
		getitem 7416,1;
		close;
	}
	else if(mao_request == 1)
	{

	if((Class == Job_Assassin) || (Class == Job_Assassin_Cross))
	{
		if(mao_request == 1)
		{
			mes "[Jack]";
			mes "I've been waiting for";
			mes "you. Erm, why don't you";
			mes "go inside? Ah, this must";
			mes "be your first time here.";
			next;
			mes "[Jack]";
			mes "Hey, you shouldn't worry,";
			mes "this bar is just for people";
			mes "like us. Besides, you'll be";
			mes "coming more often from now";
			mes "on. Anyway, the Bar Master";
			mes "is waiting for you inside.";
			close;
		}
		else if(mao_request > 1)
		{
			mes "[Jack]";
			mes "Hey, it looks like";
			mes "you've been keeping";
			mes "busy. Good for you~";
			mes "Hey, I'll see you around.";
			close;
		}
		else
		{
			mes "[Jack]";
			mes "Whoa, whoa...";
			mes "Wait. I dunno if I can";
			mes "let you in just yet. Ah,";
			mes "whatever, you're one of";
			mes "us. If it's just for a drink,";
			mes "I shouldn't get in trouble...";
			close;
		}
	}
	if(mao_request == 1 && countitem(7416))
	{
		mes "[Jack]";
		mes "Oh, hey, you must be the";
		mes "one I've been waiting for.";
		mes "Yeah, alright, come on in,";
		mes "and don't forget to show";
		mes "the letter of recommendation";
		mes "to the Bar Master, okay?";
		close;
	}
	else if(mao_request > 1)
	{
		mes "[Jack]";
		mes "It's a little weird since";
		mes "you're not really part of";
		mes "our guild, but you're allowed";
		mes "to enter our secret hideaway";
		mes "from now on. But don't you";
		mes "dare tell anybody about this!";
		close;
	}
	else
	{
		mes "[Jack]";
		mes "What? I don't have";
		mes "anything to talk to";
		mes "you about. Move along,";
		mes "adventurer, and don't";
		mes "bother me anymore.";
		close;
	}
}

	donpcevent "#maobar6::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Marjana#poison::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#mao_table::OnInit";
	$@maobar_room = 0;
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

	donpcevent "#maobar6::OnEnter";
	end;
	
OnTimer245000:
	donpcevent "#maobar6::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#1::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#2::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Marjana#poison::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#mao_table::OnInit";
	end;
	
OnTimer250000:
	mapannounce "que_job01","The security magic in the Master Zone, Area 1 is deactivated.",1,0x70DBDB;
	$@maobar_room = 0;
	stopnpctimer;
	end;
}

	donpcevent "#maobar7::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#maobar8::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#Rabsent::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#mao_empty::OnInit";
	$@maobar_room2 = 0;
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

	donpcevent "#maobar7::OnEnter";
	donpcevent "#maobar8::OnEnter";
	end;

	donpcevent "#maobar7::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#maobar8::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Valdes#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Lin#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "Kidd#3::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#Rabsent::OnInit";
	donpcevent "#mao_empty::OnInit";
	end;
	
OnTimer250000:
	mapannounce "que_job01","Security Level in the Master Zone, Area 2 deactivated.",1,0x70DBDB;
	$@maobar_room2 = 0;
	stopnpctimer;
	end;
}

que_job03,122,106,1	script	#maogate2_end2	139,15,15,{

OnInit:
	disablenpc "#maogate2_end2";
	end;
	
OnEnter:
	enablenpc "#maogate2_end2";
	end;

OnTouch:
	if (mao_request == 126)
	{
		cutin "mocseal_kid01.bmp",2;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [Kidd]";
		mes "" + strcharinfo(0) + "...!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Can you hear me? Oh man...";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] You don't look so hot. Come";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] on, we gotta get you back";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to the guild for now...";
		set mao_request,127;
		close2;
		mapwarp "que_job03","que_job01",59,49;
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk1::OnInit";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk2::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk3::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk4::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk5::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk6::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_talk7::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "Kidd#maogate2_1::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Kidd#maogate2_2::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Lin#maogate2_1::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Lin#maogate2_2::OnInit";
		donpcevent "R#maogate2::OnInit";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_end::OnStop";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_end::OnInit";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_end2::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Dandelion#maogate2_1::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Dandelion#maogate2_2::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Dandelion#maogate2_3::OnInit";
		donpcevent "Dandelion#maogate2_4::OnInit";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_setting::OnEnter";
		donpcevent "Dandelion Member#2_bt::OnInit";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_battle::OnStop";
		donpcevent "#maogate2_battle::OnEnter";
		enablenpc "#maogate2";
		set $mao_gate2,0;
		end;
	}
}

morocc,30,29,5	script	Member#mao1	880,10,15,{

	mes "[DRY-RUN] [Chairman]";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] So it's agreed.";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] Tomorrow we'll clean";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] the pond near the south";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] gate tomorrow. I hope";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] that everyone can make it.";
	next;
	mes "[DRY-RUN] [Members]";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] Sure, no problem.";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] When are we planning";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] on reconstructing the";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] daycare facilities?";
	next;
	mes "[DRY-RUN] [Chairman]";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] Hmmm...";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] I guess that's an";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] issue that we can";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] save for tomorrow's";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] meeting. I'll see you then.";
	next;
	mes "["+ strcharinfo(0) +"]";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] Is this some";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] sort of volunteer";
	mes "[DRY-RUN] service group?";
	close;

OnStop:
	disablenpc "Member#mao1";
	end;
	
OnEnter:
	enablenpc "Member#mao1";
	end;
	
OnTouch:
	if (mao_request == 30 || mao_request == 128)
	{
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [?????]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ...That's what";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] happened... Worked";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] hard... This time...";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [???]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] There is just one";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] regret... Was that...";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ...tan... was... better...";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [????????]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] I know, I know that!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] But we still accomplished";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] what we set out to do, right?";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [??????]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Quiet!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] You're too loud.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [?????]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] I'm pretty sure...";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] ...is... not going to";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] be quiet about this.";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Perhaps... it'll happen.";
		next;
		mes "[DRY-RUN] [???]";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Shh. Act naturally!";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] Someone's listening";
		mes "[DRY-RUN] to us! Get out of here!";
		close2;
		donpcevent "Member#mao1::OnStop";
		donpcevent "Member#mao2::OnStop";
		donpcevent "Member#mao3::OnStop";
		donpcevent "Member#mao4::OnStop";
		if($maoattack > 49)
		{
			donpcevent "#mao_manager::OnStart";
			set $maoattack,0;
		}
		else donpcevent "#mao_timer::OnStart";
		end;
	}
}

	end;

que_job01,70,84,1	duplicate(Simon#mao)	Kimmie	882

sec_in02,38,162,0	script	Morocc Invasion Manager	882,{
	callfunc "F_GM_NPC";
	mes "A total of " + $maoattack + " users completed";
	mes "the Satan Morocc: Lin Quest.";
	mes "There are 2 requirements to";
	mes "summon Satan Morocc's troops.";
	mes "1) 50 users must complete";
	mes "this Satan Morocc: Lin Quest.";
	next;
	mes "2) One of these users that";
	mes "completed the Lin Quest must";
	mes "approach the Dandelion Org";
	mes "NPCs at the outskirts of Morocc to trigger the monster invasion.";
	mes "Change the GlobalVar to affect status of Satan Morocc invasion?";
	next;
	switch( select( "Set Globalvar","Cancel" ) )
	{
		case 1:
			mes "Please choose the number";
			mes "of times that the Lin Quest";
			mes "will be recorded as completed";
			mes "on the server. 0 is essentially";
			mes "a reset; 50 will immediately";
			mes "make the invasion available.";
			next;
			switch( select( "49","50","0" ) )
			{
				case 1:
					mes "The GlobalVar has been";
					mes "set to 49. The Lin Quest";
					mes "must be completed 1 more";
					mes "time before the Satan Morocc";
					mes "invasion can be triggered.";
					set $maoattack,49;
					close;

				case 2:
					mes "The GlobalVar has been";
					mes "set to 50. The Satan Morocc";
					mes "invasion can now be triggered.";
					set $maoattack,50;
					close;
				
				case 3:
					mes "The GlobalVar has been";
					mes "set to 0. The Lin Quest";
					mes "must be completed 1 more";
					mes "time before the Satan Morocc";
					mes "invasion can be triggered.";
					set $maoattack,0;
					close;
			}

		case 2:
			mes "You have canceled.";
			close;
	}
}
